## Race-by-Race ELO Changes

### Round 1: Argentine Grand Prix
*Date: 1958-01-19*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 8: German Grand Prix
*Date: 1958-08-03*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
